Unfortunately, due to the pandemic laws, the shop was not allowed to ship to me nor was I able to go and pickup curbside. So, in April I reached out to Stephen to find out if he'd ship. It seemed ridiculous to buy from a shop all the way on the other side of the country, but I'm glad that I did. Not only could I help a friend, not only could I support a small owner run business, but I appreciated Stephen's passion and work ethic. Let me tell you a brief story - the place I mention above that's here in NYC has a great selection and I really like the guy who runs it, but they fail at followup. I've had to chase them multiple times to order things and simply respond to emails. In two days they were in my hand. Now that's a good businessman and anyone who can follow up better than me has my respect and my business. Going forward, as long as it makes sense to continue buying from a store 3000 miles away, I will. BTW the issues showed up in pristine condition. <userid>104745565929433688409< /userid><name>Ken Mann</name><date>1573962134553</date>< rate>
5<//rate>
< text>
Get ready to be enchanted.  This is one of the finest restaurants anywhere.  They have everything right.  And not one ingredient is in its original form - something creative has made each one special - even the garnishes.

A warm welcoming decor that's casual and elegant all at once.  The personnel introduce themselves without the "I'm your waiter Bob" line and not necessarily on the encounter.

I ordered a Pisco Sour, the national drink of Peru.  Pisco (a Peruvian Brandy), lemon juice, simple syrup and then egg whites that provide a smooth foam.  On par with the best I've had in Lima.

Then to the yellowtail ceviche.  Perfectly cut, not a hint of connective tissue and a sublime marinade with tiger milk, sliced red onion and nuts to add some crunch.  Beautifully served in glazed handmade pottery.

On to Panacota for dessert.  Add toasted quinoa sprinkled on top and have it sit in fermented honey, then artfully place pieces of what they call "Forest" on top.  They look like shaved bark, they have some crunch and the taste is mildly sweet and savory - a wonderful accompaniment to the not overly sweet dish.

Bottom line.  A winner any way you want to measure a restaurant.</text>

< text>
I am Power of Attorney for my father who is a client of Stockton Rescue Mission in Stockton. They serve as his Payee. Just recently I brought my father home to live with me, he require 24 hour care. I set up a care provider to be with my father while I was at work. Because my father is not eligible for IHSS we both have to pay the provider out of our pocket. My father has a VA pension along with Social security. I pay for half the providers hours, and my father the other half. I send in invoice to the Payee and time card to the payee on that time card it shows the amount I pay and the amount my father is to pay. The payee said she sent the check for the care provider out on a Wednesday,. We live in Elk Grove, come Friday, I informed her the check had not arrived, she said it will be there. come that following Monday the check still hadn't arrived. The care provider was beginning to worry about his pay. Come Tuesday the check still had not arrived. I contacted the payee and informed her the check still had not arrived and I would like to pick the check up for the care provider in order for him to continue working with my father as I work. I work in Stockton and it would have been no problem to pick the check up. She in turn told me she cannot issue another check. I asked her, to please put a stop payment on the "check" you sent out and re-issue another check. I informed her this could be really bad, because the care provider is threatening not to continue work if he is not paid. I also informed her, I was unable to take off anymore days from work, or it could cause me to loose my job. She didn't care. She never responded back again. I tried calling her several times, I text her, and I sent out emails to her, to no avail. She never responded back. When I went home that night, I had to show the care provider that I was really trying to get his pay. I showed him the emails and the text messages that I sent. By the grace of God he agreed to come back the next day.
The next morning as I was heading to work, I received a call from the care provider informing me that the Payee called him and informed him that the check was mailed out, she also informed him that I wanted her to put the check in my name which was a flat out lie. As my fathers Power of Attorney, in which I supplied a copy of the Power of Attorney to the Gospel Rescue Mission in Stockton, directly to his payee, I speak for my father. My father has several different disabilities including Parkinson and sever  psychological  disabilities. The payee is very much aware of this. She still did not put my father's best interest first. She didn't care if we lost the care provider, she didn't care if I lost my job because my father cannot be left alone. She just didn't care. When I realized this, I began looking for a new payee service for my father. I removing his services from this place, because they clearly don't care about the client well being.<//text>

<Name>Andii Lee</Name><time>1555362615059</time><rating>2< /rating>< Text>
Average car wash, with a side of mismanagement...and verbal abuse.

Today (4/15) around 1pm I took my car in to get gas/wash, received my ticket from an employee who confirmed make/model/color of my car, and headed to the register.

While in line, Rob (the manager working at the gas pumps) walks in screaming at me that I took someone else's ticket, that he had called out another car and I took a ticket from him by mistake (untrue). Takes the ticket from my hand, I follow him outside and there's now more than 3 customers (myself included) waiting while he yells at me explaining that a Highlander and CR-V are two different cars. Swaps tickets between several customers and walks off.

I take the new ticket to the register and am given the total after my card is charged - over $20 more than possible for the size of my gas tank. I tell the cashier and he says I'd have to go back and get a different ticket. I told him I don't want to go back out and get screamed at by Rob so I'll pay the extra and be done with it.

Congrats to the lucky customer who got a cheap tank of gas, I paid the difference on yours. I hope that Rob gets placed in a role where he isn't working with customers.

I've been a customer of Educated for over 10 years, and they have a reliable service, sometimes exceptional, other times average. Cannot beat the convenience of having your gas/car taken care of while you relax. After today, I don't think I'll ever go back. It's not worth being screamed at and treated this poorly.<//Text>

< review>
I have been going there for over 25 years and have always been happy with the service. However, things change and not always for the better. I'm not sure what has changed, but the quality of the service has definitely gone down(a very steep) hill. I have had to really check the car out recently - the fenders weren't washed, the windows had streaks. The final straw was two day ago. When I went to look at the car, the usual mud had not been washed off the front. But worse, the hood looked like it had been smeared with some kind of goo. I went to the cashier who couldn't find the front manager, so said I needed to find the manage who was in the back. Well, he was busy but would be there "soon". I went back to my car and waited. After 5 minutes, the front manager came out. I started to show him the problem when the back manager showed up. I started to explain the problem and one of them said "now cool down, we'll fix the problem." Well at that point, I wasn't angry, but when I pointed out the condition of the hood and that it looked worse now than when I brought it in, all they could say was "that's not our problem, it need to be waxed." I said that it didn't look that bad when I brought it in. "Well we couldn't do that". It was like being in the movie "Dumb and Dumber". What about these spots on the hood? "We can't get those off."
Like I said, I have been going there for over 25 years. But no more. I know enough about cars to know that they could have cleaned it but did not. And they were just too lazy to run it through again. I took it home and washed it myself and it came out fine. This is a sad case of what used to be a good place has gone down hill.
Go some place else, shoddy work should not be rewarded.</review>
